def get_ncaab_schedule():
    """NCAAB Schedule - Update once per season"""
    # ------ Enter NCAAB schedule code here ------
    ncaab_schedule = [
        # Add your NCAAB games here
        # Example:
        # {
        #     'match_id': 1,
        #     'round': 1,
        #     'date': '2024-11-04',
        #     'venue': 'Arena Name',
        #     'home_team': 'Team Name',
        #     'away_team': 'Team Name',
        #     'result': None
        # },
    ]
    # ------------------------------------------
    return ncaab_schedule

def get_wnba_schedule():
    """WNBA Schedule - Update once per season"""
    # ------ Enter WNBA schedule code here ------
    wnba_schedule = [
        # Add your WNBA games here
        # Example:
        # {
        #     'match_id': 1,
        #     'round': 1,
        #     'date': '2024-05-14',
        #     'venue': 'Arena Name',
        #     'home_team': 'Team Name',
        #     'away_team': 'Team Name',
        #     'result': None
        # },
    ]
    # ------------------------------------------
    return wnba_schedule

# Schedule getter functions mapping
SCHEDULE_FUNCTIONS = {
    'NFL': get_nfl_schedule,
    'NBA': get_nba_schedule,
    'NHL': get_nhl_schedule,
    'MLB': get_mlb_schedule,
    'NCAAF': get_ncaaf_schedule,
    'NCAAB': get_ncaab_schedule,
    'WNBA': get_wnba_schedule
}

def get_schedule(sport_code):
    """
    Get schedule for a specific sport.
    
    Args:
        sport_code: Sport code (e.g., 'NFL', 'NBA', 'NHL', etc.)
    
    Returns:
        List of dictionaries containing schedule data
    """
    if sport_code not in SCHEDULE_FUNCTIONS:
        return None
    
    return SCHEDULE_FUNCTIONS[sport_code]()

def get_available_sports():
    """Get list of sports with available schedules."""
    available = []
    for sport_code, func in SCHEDULE_FUNCTIONS.items():
        schedule = func()
        if schedule and len(schedule) > 0:
            available.append(sport_code)
    return available

if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Test the schedules
    print("Available sports with schedules:")
    for sport in get_available_sports():
        schedule = get_schedule(sport)
        print(f"  {sport}: {len(schedule)} games")
